 inakam tex bachaane ke liye makaan kiraaya bhatta, yani house rent elouns (echaare) ek aisa mad he, jo aapako sabase zyaada madad de saktaa he, or bahut-se naukareepesha log iskaa istemaal bhi karte hai
 
 
 To save income tax, many employed people get income tax exemption on that amount by paying rent to their parents, but they need to keep some things in mind
 
 
 darasal, inakam tex act ke section 10 (13 e) ke tahat kisi bhi vetanbhogi ko echaare main uske mul vetan kaa 50 fisadi, echaare ke mad main milane vaali rakam yaa chukaaye gaye vaastavik kiraaye main se mul vetan kaa 10 fisadi ghataane par bachi rakam main se sabase kam rakam par iskar se chhot milti he, so, bahut-se naukareepesha apni maa yaa pita ke naam kiraaye kii raseeden dekar chhot hasil kar lete hai
 
 
 The most important thing to keep in mind for them is that the mother or father is also required to pay tax on this rent by showing it in their income
 
 
 
 
 
 And more importantly, the house that the employed person is claiming to pay should not be named after him
 
 
 tippaniyan For example, if a person receives Rs
 50,000 as basic salary, and Rs
 25,000 under the head of HRA, and he actually pays Rs
 25,000, then he will be able to get a rebate of Rs
 20,000 only because the repayment
 This amount is saved by deducting 10% of the basic salary from the amount of rental
 
 
 lekin ab yaad rakhane vaali baat yah he ki kiraaya vasuul karne vaale maa yaa pita kii aay 20,000 rupee masik bad jaaegi (yadi unki aay shunya he, to bhi ab unki aay 20,000 rupee masik maani jaaegi), or is rakam par unhen inakam tex dena hi hoga
 
 
 So, it is important that the house is not the property of the renter, and the rent paid to the mother or father should be given through the bank, and the rent collector (mother or father) will get income on the amount received as rent

 udhaaharan ke liye, yadi kisi vyakti ko 50,000 rupee mul vetan ke rup main praapt hote hai, or 25,000 rupee echaare ke mad main, or vah 25,000 rupee hi vastav main kiraaya detaa he, to use 20,000 rupee par hi chhot mil paaegi, kyonki chukaaye gaye kiraaye kii rakam main se mul vetan kaa 10 fisadi ghataane par yahi rakam bachati he

 ) The demand for scooters is increasing in the Indian market

 isamen sudhaar laate hue companiyon ne electric opshan bhi tri kiya he
 We are going to tell you about some selected scooters that are going to knock in India in some time
 1
 Ather S340 This scooter is a product of Ather Energy, a startup company in India, discovered in 2013 by Tarun Mehta and Swapnil Jain, alumni of IIT Madras
 Ather S340 vaise to ek electric scooter hi he lekin aam scootaron se kaaphi alag he isamen andvanced technology kaa upyog kiya gaya he
 The company claims that it is a 90 percent Made in India product
 keval iske lithium aayan bydaree ko hi baahar se mangavaya gaya he
 It has two riding modes Economy and Sport
 company ke daawey ke mutabik isaki top speed 72 kmph he
 It can be charged up to 80 percent through fast charging support within 1 hour
 2
 Hero Duet e This is the concept model of the Duet scooter currently on sale
 Hero Duet e jo ki puri tarah se ek electric scooter he ise 2016 auto expo ke dauraan pesh kiya gaya tha
 This e-scooter has an electric motor that produces torque of 5 Kw and 14 Nm
 company ke daawey ke mutabik ye 0-60 kmph kii speed 6
 Goes away in 5 seconds
 iske alaava ye scooter single charge main hi 65 km tak chal saktaa he
 3
 TVS entorq 125TVS motor company ne 2016 auto expo ke dauraan ek special scooter kaa concept pesh kiya tha, jiskaa naam company ne TVS entorq 210 rakhaa tha

 haalanki ye jald hi production ke liye jayega

 TVS Entorq 210 ke saath saath ummid ke mutabik TVS isi concept par besd ek production ready 125 cc varjan entorq 125 ko pesh kar sakati he
 4
 Vespa GTS 300italian manufacturer Piaggio bharat main ek premium scooter Vespa GTS 300 kii taiyaari kar rahaa he
 According to its price, it will not be difficult to say that it will be one of the most expensive scooters sold in India
 khabar ye bhi he ki bharat main isaki kamplitaly bilt unit pesh kii jaaegi
 That is, fully made units will be brought for sale in India
 ise retro dizin main taiyaar kiya gaya he
 The Vespa GTS 300 has a 278 cc single cylinder engine which is 21 bhp and 22
 3 Nm kaa pick tork generat karata he
 It has an LCD display
 international market main is scooter main tranjaction control or dual channel ABS diya gaya he
 The most important thing that is associated with this scooter is its price
 isaki exshorum keemtakareeb 4 lakh rupeke aas paas rahegi
 In such a situation, it will be very interesting to see if the customers adopt this scooter at this price
 company ne isse bhi mahangi scooter taiyaar kii he Vespa 946 Emporio Armani jisaki ekssho rum keemat lagbhag 12 lakh rupee hogi
 5
 Hero ZIRZIR 150 ke jariye Hero motocorp 150CC scooter segment main entry lene ja rahi he
 The ZIR 150 will compete with the Honda PCX 150
 jo videshon main bikne ke baad bharat main pair pasaarne ja rahi he

 jo do vairient flat floorboard or European style step-through main aegi

 8 bhp kaa power or 12
